private void DialogAdd(){

final RadioButton RbtnMale=(RadioButton) dialog.findViewById(R.id.RbtnMale);
RadioButton RbtnFemale=(RadioButton) dialog.findViewById(R.id.RbtnFemale);
final EditText inputPhone=(EditText) dialog.findViewById(R.id.inputPhone);
final EditText inputAddress=(EditText) dialog.findViewById(R.id.inputAddress);

btnDelete.setEnabled(false);

@Override

String Address=inputAddress.getText().toString().trim();

dialog.cancel();
GetDataSV();
}
}
});
dialog.show();
}
